[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work with 7 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here's how I structured this JSON:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "CODE":"STRESS_AT_WORK",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "TYPE_ID":3,
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                    
                 }
             ]
}
```

Now, let's fill in the questionnaire with 7 questions:

```json
{
    "data": 
        {  
            _TF_QUESTIONNAIRES:
                [
                   {
                      CODE: 'STRESS_AT_WORK',
                     NAME:'Stress at Work Questionnaire',   
                    TYPE_ID :3,
                  "_TF_QUESTIONS":
                        [    
                          {"CODE":"Q1",  "NAME":"'Do you feel stressed when your workload is heavy?'",
                            "TYPE_ID":2, 
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:0,"_tf_answers":[{"ANSWER':'Yes'},{"Answer ':'No'}]},

                         {   CODE:" Q2","Name ":"How often do you experience stress at work?" ,
                          TYPE_ID :1,
                        'DISPLAY ORDER': 3,' _TF_ANSWERS' [{' ANSWER :'Daily'},
                                            {'AnsweR:','Weekly'}
                                           ]},
                       {"CODE":"Q5", "NAME":"'Do your colleagues or supervisor ever ask for something that causes you stress?'",
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:4,"_tf_answers":[{"ANSWER':'Yes'},{"Answer ':'No'}]},

                        {   CODE:" Q6","Name ":"Have there been times when work-related issues have caused significant emotional distress?" ,
                          TYPE_ID :1,
                         'DISPLAY ORDER': 5,' _TF_ANSWERS' [{' ANSWER :'True'},
                                            {'AnsweR:','False'}
                                           ]},
                       {"CODE":"Q7", "NAME":"'Do you feel that your job is a source of stress in life?'",
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:6,"_tf_answers":[{"ANSWER':'Yes'},{"Answer ':'No'}]},

                        ]
                    }
                ]

        }

```

This questionnaire contains 2 multiple-choice questions, one rating question and four single-answer choice.

Here's your Workplace Environment Questionnaire with 7 questions:
```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                  "CODE":"WORKPLACE_ENVIRONMENT",
                   "NAME":"",
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[

                        // Q1: How satisfied are you overall about the workplace environment?
                          {"code" : 123456, 
                           "name" :"How would rate your satisfaction with our work place?",
                            "type_id":3,
                             "display_order":"0",
                              '_tf_answers':[
                                  {'answer':"Very Satisfied"},
                                   { 'answe':"Satisified"}
                               ]
                          },
                        // Q2: Do you feel comfortable sharing ideas and opinions in the workplace?
                           {"code" : 123457, 
                            "name":"
Do yuo find it easy to share your thoughts?",
                             "type_id":"1",
                              "_tf_answers":[
                                  {'answer':"Yes"},
                                   { 'answe':"No"}
                               ]
                          },
                        // Q3: How often do you feel stressed at work?
                           {"code" : 123458, 
                            "name":"
How offten are yoou feeling stresed?",
                             "_tf_answers":[
                                  {'answer':"Often"},
                                   { 'answe':"Rarely"}
                               ]
                          },
                        // Q4: Do your colleagues support you in times when needed?
                           {"code" : 123459, 
                            "name":"
Do yuo feel that yoour collaugues are suppoorting",
                             "_tf_answers":[
                                  {'answer':"Yes"},
                                   { 'answe':"No"}
                               ]
                          },
                        // Q5: Are there enough opportunities for professional development in the workplace?
                           {"code" : 123460, 
                            "name":"
Do yuo think ther are enought oppotunities",
                             "_tf_answers":[
                                  {'answer':"Yes"},
                                   { 'answe':"No"}
                               ]
                          },
                        // Q6: Do you feel valued and recognized for your contributions to the organization?

Do yuo feal that yoour contributios are valud",
                             "_tf_answers":[
                                  {'answer':"Yes"},

                               ]
                          },
                        // Q7: Do you think the workplace environment is conducive to innovation and creativity?

Do yuo thnk that yoour work place",

Here is the generated questionnaire on End of working relationship with 10 questions:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                  "CODE":"END_OF_WORKING_RELATIONSHIP",
                   "NAME":"",
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[ 
                        {  
                          " CODE ":"Q1",   
                           " NAME ":"
How would you rate the overall experience of working with this employee?",    
                            " TYPE_ID":3,     
                             " DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_" TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Excellent' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Good'
                               }]
                        },
                        
                         {  
                          CODE ":"Q2",   
                           NAME ":"
What was the primary reason for ending this working relationship?",    
                            TYPE_ID":1,     
                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Poor performance' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Lack of skills'
                               }]
                        },
                        
                         {  
                          CODE ":"Q3",   
                           NAME ":"
How would you rate the employee's communication style?",    
                            TYPE_ID":1,     
                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Clear and concise' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Unclear'
                               }]
                        },
                        
                         {  
                          CODE ":"Q4",   
                           NAME ":"
What steps could have been taken to improve the working relationship?",    
                            TYPE_ID":2,     
                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Provide additional training' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Offer more support'
                               }]
                        },
                        
                         {  
                          CODE ":"Q5",   
                           NAME ":"
How would you rate the employee's teamwork and collaboration skills?",    
                            TYPE_ID":1,     
                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Excellent' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Good'
                               }]
                        },
                        
                         {  
                          CODE ":"Q6",   
                           NAME ":"
What do you think the employee's strengths and weaknesses are?",    
                            TYPE_ID":2,     
                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,
                              "_TF_ANSWERS "[{ ANSWER: 'Strengths - attention to detail; Weaknesses- lack of initiative' }, {
                                ANSWEAR :'Other'
                               }]
                        },

How would you rate the employee's adaptability and flexibility?",

                             DISPLAY_ORDER" : 0,

                                ANSWEAR :'Good'
                               }]
                        },

                               }]

[LLM ANSWER]

```json
{
    "data": {
        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "CODE":"ONBOARDING",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "TYPE_ID":3,
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],

Here is the generated questionnaire on Onboarding with 6 questions:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                  CODE: ONBOARDING, 
                   NAME:"On-Boarding Questionnaire",  
                    TYPE_ID :3,
                     _TF_QUESTIONS:
                        [   
                            {CODE :"Q1",
                              name :'How would you rate the overall onboarding experience at our company?',
                               type_id 2,'DESCRIPTION': 'Use this scale to evaluate your new hire journey: Very Good, Average or Needs Improvement.'},
                             {
                                CODE:" Q2", 
                                 NAME:'What aspects of training and orientation were most helpful in getting started with work?',  
                                  TYPE_ID :1,
                                   _TF_ANSWERS:
                                       [
                                          {ANSWER :'Job-specific skills'},
                                          
                                         ]
                                     },
                            {CODE :"Q3",
                              name  'How would you rate the level of support from your supervisor or HR during onboarding?',
                               type_id:2,'DESCRIPTION': 
                                "Please use this scale to evaluate their helpfulness, Very Good (5), Average(4) , Needs Improvement'(1-3)."},
                             {
                                 CODE:"Q4",  
                                  NAME:'What changes would you suggest making in the current process of onboarding new employees?',   
                                   TYPE_ID :6,'DESCRIPTION': 
                                    "Please rate each option from 0 to 10. (e.g., 'More training sessions' =7, etc.)"},
                            {CODE :"Q5",
                              name :'Would like any additional support or resources during the first few weeks of employment? If yes please specify.',  
                               type_id:4,'DESCRIPTION': 
                                "Please provide your feedback in a text box."},
                             {
                                 CODE:" Q6",   
                                  NAME:'Any other comments, suggestions about onboarding process?',    
                                   TYPE_ID :5,
                                    _TF_ANSWERS:
                                        [
                                            {ANSWER :'More time for training'},
                                            
                                          ]
                                      }
                            ] 
                        }  
                    ],
                },
            ],        
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gauge the effectiveness of your company's On-Boarding process and provide valuable feedback from new hires.

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Employee feedback with 4 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]

    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "_CODE_QUESTIONS":"EmployeeFeedback",
                    "__NAME__" :   "Your Feedback Matters!",
                    
                     '_TYPE_ID_' 3,
                    
                        _questions_: 
                            [  
                                {   
                                    'code':     '',
                                     '__name'__:    '',    
                                        TYPE:       ,        
                                            DISPLAY_ORDER',        ,
                                             ANSWERS_ [
                                         ]
                                 },
                                  {
                                      code:'',
                                       __NAME__ :   ''     
                                          type 4,
                                           display_order,      
                                              answers [ 
                                                  {ANSWER''},
                                                  
                                               ]   
                                    }
                                }            
                            ]

```

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Training to professional users with 12 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here's how I structured this JSON:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "_CODE_QUESTIONS":"TRAINING",
                    "*NAME_*" :   "Training for Professional Users Questionnaire", 
                     *_TYPE_ID_: 3,  
                      _*_ QUESTIONS: [   
                        {"code_question1","What do you think is the most important aspect of training in your role?"},
                          {type_id":2,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Content"},{"Answer ":"Format"}]},
                         "display_order" :   0, 
                      },  
                    {
                       code_question:    {"code_question1","How would you rate the effectiveness of our current training programs?"},   
                        type_:            {type_id":3,"MIN_VALUE_5.00",MAX VALUE_"10.000"},    
                         _TF_ANSWERS_[{ANSWER":"Very Effective"}],{"Answer ":"Somewhat effective" }, {"answer :"Not VeryEffective","answering "not at alleffective""}, 
                        display_order:     1,  
                    },
                   {
                       code_question:"How do you currently stay up-to-date with industry developments and trends?",   
                         type_:            {type_id":2,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Online Courses"},{"Answer ":"Conferences" }, {"answer :"Books"} , 
                        display_order:     3,  
                    },
                   {
                       code_question:"Have you ever experienced any difficulties or challenges while using our training materials?",   
                         type_:            {type_id":1,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Yes"},{"Answer ":"No" }],    
                          "display order ":   ,4,
                     }, 
                  {"code question:    How do think we could improve the overall quality of your learning experience?"},
                    {
                        "_CODE_QUESTION_" : 5,   
                         type_:            {type_id":2,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"More Interactive Content"},{"Answer ":"Better Navigation" } , 
                          "display_order ":   },6,
                     },
                   {"code_question:    What do you think is the most significant barrier to your ability to learn and apply new skills?"},
                    {
                        "_CODE_QUESTION_" : 7,   
                         type_:            {type_id":1,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Lack of Time"},{"Answer ":"Insufficient Resources" } , 
                          "display_order ":   },8,
                     },
                   {"code_question:    How do you currently prioritize your learning and professional development?"},
                    {
                        "_CODE_QUESTION_" : 9,   
                         type_:            {type_id":2,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Self-Directed"},{"Answer ":"Formal Education" } , 
                          "display_order ":   },10,
                     },
                   {"code_question:    Have you ever received any feedback on your performance or skills from our training programs?"},
                    {
                        "_CODE_QUESTION_" : 11,   
                         type_:            {type_id":1,"_TF_ANSWERS":[{"ANSWER":"Yes"},{"Answer ":"No" }],    
                          "display_order ":   },12,
                     },
                ]
              }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather information from professional users about their training experiences and preferences. The 12 questions cover various aspects of the topic, including what they think are important in a learning experience (Q1), how effective current programs have been for them personally(Q2).

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000003
     - Topic: Employee potential
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100004
     - Topic: Access to Technology and Tools
     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools with 9 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here's how I structured this JSON:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "CODE":"ACCESS_TO_TECHNOLOGY",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                    
                
}
```

Here is the generated questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools with 9 questions:

```json
{

        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100009
     - Topic: Career Path Clarity
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

                   "NAME":"",
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[

                           NAME:"What motivates you to achieve your career goals?",
                            TYPE_ID : 4,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":"Personal growth and development"},
                                 {'ANSWER':'Financial stability'},
                                  {'ANswer':"Sense of accomplishment"}
                               ]
                        },
                         {  
                          CODE: 'Q2',
                           NAME:"How often do you think about your long-term career goals?",
                            TYPE_ID : 1,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":"Daily"},
                                 {'ANswer':"Weekly"}
                               ]
                        },
                         {  
                          CODE: 'Q3',
                           NAME:"Do any specific industries or job roles interest you? If so please specify.",
                            TYPE_ID : 2,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":""},
                                 {'ANswer':''}
                               ]
                        },
                         {  
                          CODE: 'Q4',
                           NAME:"What skills do you think are essential for your ideal career path?",
                            TYPE_ID :6 ,  // Distribute weights across several items/options
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":"Communication"},
                                 {'ANswer':"Problem-solving"}
                               ]
                        },
                         {  
                          CODE: 'Q5',
                           NAME:"How important is it for you to have a clear career path?",
                            TYPE_ID : 1,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[

                                 {'ANanswer':"Somewhat Importance"}
                               ]
                        },
                         {

                           NAME:"What steps are you currently taking to achieve your career goals?",
                            TYPE_ID : 4,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":"Networking"},
                                 {'ANanswer':"Taking courses"}
                               ]
                        },
                         {  
                          CODE: 'Q7',
                           NAME:"What obstacles do you think might hinder your progress towards achieving career goals?",
                            TYPE_ID : 2,
                             DISPLAY_ORDER":0, 
                              '_TF_ANSWERS':[
                                {"ANSWER":"Lack of resources"},
                                 {'ANanswer':"Fear"}
                               ]
                        }
                    ]  
                }   
            ],
        "TYPE_ID" :3
    },
}

Here is the generated employee motivational survey in json format:
JSON Format for Employee Motivation Questionnaire with 5 questions
The root of our questionnaire object contains a single property 'DATA'. The DATA has one more level, which represents an array called TF_QUESTIONNAIRES. This includes only ONE element that stands as this specific questionnare.
```
{
    "data": {
        "TF QUESTIONNAIRS":
            [
                {
                    "CODE" : 1,
                    "NAME":"Employee Motivation Questionnaire",
                    "_TYPE_ID_ ":3, 
                    
                    // Here are the questions
                     _QUESTIONS_:[
                        {" CODE ":"Q001",  
                         " NAME":   "Do you feel motivated to come into work every day?",   
                          TYPE ID" : 1,
                           DISPLAY ORDER:0 ,    
                            ANSWERS:[
                                {ANSWER:"Strongly Agree"},
                                 
                               ]
                             },
                        
                       // Question2
                        {" CODE ":"Q002",  
                         NAME":   "Do you feel like your efforts are recognized and valued by the organization?",   
                          TYPE ID" : 1,
                           DISPLAY ORDER:0 ,    
                            ANSWERS:[
                                {ANSWER:"Strongly Agree"},
                                 
                               ]
                             },
                        
                       // Question3
                        {" CODE ":"Q003",  
                         NAME":   "How would you rate your job satisfaction level on a scale of (5) where ' 1' is very low and '(4)'is high?",   
                          TYPE ID" :2,
                           DISPLAY ORDER:0 ,    
                            ANSWERS:[
                                {ANSWER:"Very Low"},
                                 
                               ]
                             },
                        
                       // Question4
                        {" CODE ":"Q004",  
                         NAME":   "Do you feel like your skills are being utilized effectively in the organization?",   
                          TYPE ID" :1,
                           DISPLAY ORDER:0 ,    
                            ANSWERS:[
                                {ANSWER:"Strongly Agree"},
                                 
                               ]
                             },
                        
                       // Question5
                        {" CODE ":"Q005",  
                         NAME":   "Would you recommend this company as a great place to work?",   
                          TYPE ID" :1,
                           DISPLAY ORDER:0 ,    
                            ANSWERS:[
                                {ANSWER:"Strongly Agree"},
                                 
                               ]
                             },
                        
                    ]

                }
            ]



}
```

Please note that the actual data in your JSON file will be different from this example.

            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100028
     - Topic: Kick-off Meeting Feedback
     - Question number: 7

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Kick-off Meeting Feedback with 7 questions

```Json

"data" : {

   "Tf_questionnaires":

    [

      { 

         _code: 'KickoffMeetingFeedback', 
        name:'Kick-Off meeting - Your thoughts and suggestions',
       type_id :'3' , // TYPE_ID = Kick-off Meeting Feedback
       
 "_tf_questions": [
    
     {
        
          code : 1,  
           Name:"How would you rate the overall effectiveness of this kick-start session?",   
         Type: 'RATING', 
        display_order:'0'
      },
      
       { 

            Code :'2',
             name :"What did we do well during today's meeting? Please share your thoughts and suggestions.",    
          type_id : 1, // TYPE_ID = DESCRIPTION
           DisplayOrder:"3"
         },  
        
    {
            
              code: '4', 
               Name:'Are there any topics or areas that were not covered in the kick-off session?',   
            Type :'DESCRIPTION' ,//TYPE_DESCRIPTION= TEXTAREA
             display_order : 5
            
        },
    
       { 

           Code :"6", // TYPE_ID = DESCRIPTION, MULTIPLE CHOICE

          name: "Which of these statements best describes your overall feeling about this meeting?", 
         type_id:'2',  
        
            _tf_answers:
            
              [
                
                {
                  answer:"I am very satisfied with the outcome"
                 }, 

               {  Answer : 'The session was okay, but I have some suggestions' },
    
             ]
       } ,// TYPE_ID = DESCRIPTION

     {

        code: "7", 
         name :"Do you think this meeting has set us up for success? Why or why not?",   
      type_id :'1', //TYPE_DESCRIPTION= TEXTAREA
          display_order : 6
            
    },  
    
   {
        
            Code:"8",
             Name:'Are there any action items that were discussed during the kick-off session and need to be followed-up on?', 
        Type: 'DESCRIPTION' ,// TYPE_ID = DESCRIPTION, MULTIPLE CHOICE

         _tf_answers:
            
              [
                
                {  Answer : "Yes" },
    
               {
                  answer:"No"
                 }
             ]
       },  
        
    {

      code :'9', //TYPE_DESCRIPTION= TEXTAREA
        name: 'Any additional comments or feedback about the kick-off meeting?', 
     type_id:'1' ,// TYPE_ID = DESCRIPTION, MULTIPLE CHOICE

         display_order : 7
            
   } 

],

}

```

This questionnaire is designed to gather your thoughts and suggestions on how well you think this Kick-Off session went.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:

            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

                            "_TF_ANSWERS":

                                     {"Answer ":"Additional Compensation" },
                                     {" Answer ": "Title Change"}
                                 ]
                        },

                         // Question 3: ID, DESCRIPTION = Use this type of question to rate something.
                          TYPE_ID":1,
                           DISPLAY_ORDER":"0",
                            "_TF_ANSWERS":
                                [
                                    {ANSWER:"Not at all effective"},
                                     {"Answer ":"Somewhat Effective" },
                                     {" Answer ": "Very Effectively"}
                                 ]
                        },

                         // Question 4: ID, DESCRIPTION = Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
                          TYPE_ID":1,

                                     {"Answer ":"I don't really care" },
                                     {" Answer ": "This doesn't affect my work"}

                   {'No'}
                  ]

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100043
     - Topic: Roadmap planning feedback
     - Question number: 5
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Roadmap planning feedback with 5 questions

-------------------

                {
                    "CODE":"ROADMAP_FEEDBACK",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "TYPE_ID":3,
                   "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                    
                 }
             ]
}

                 _TF_QUESTIONS":[

                     {"CODE":"",

                       "TYPE_ID:1,DESCRIPTION:A single answer from a list.",

Here's a sample training and development programs survey with 5 questions:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                  "CODE":"TRAINING_DEVELOPMENT",
                    "NAME":"",
                   "_TF_QUESTIONS":[ 
                      {  
                        CODE:1,
                         NAME:"How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our training and development programs?",
                          TYPE_ID:3, // Rating question
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:0,

                            _TF_ANSWERS:[
                              {"ANSWER":"Very Effective"},
                               {"ANSWER": "Somewhat effective"}
                             ]
                      },
                    {
                        CODE:2,
                         NAME:"Which type(s) of training would you like to see added or improved in the future?",
                          TYPE_ID:1, // Single-select question
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:0,

                            _TF_ANSWERS:[
                              {"ANSWER":"Technical skills"},
                               {"ANSWer": "Leadership and management"}
                             ]
                      },
                    {
                        CODE:3,
                         NAME:"Have you participated in any training or development programs within the past 6 months?",
                          TYPE_ID:2, // Multi-select question
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:1,

                            _TF_ANSWERS:[
                              {"ANSWER":"Yes"},
                               {"Answer": "No"}
                             ]
                      },
                    {
                        CODE:4,
                         NAME:"What do you think is our company's greatest strength when it comes to training and development?",
                          TYPE_ID:6, // Open-ended question
                           DISPLAY_ORDER:2,

                            _TF_ANSWERS:[
                              {}
                             ]

```

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs with 8 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here's how I structured this JSON:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                    "CODE":"T&D",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[],
                    
                 }
             ]
}
```

```json

{
    "data":
        {
            "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES__":
                [
                   { 
                      CODE: TRAINING_DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAMS,
                    NAME : Training and Development Programs,  
                  TYPE_ID 3 ,   
              _TF_QUESTIONS":[
                     {"CODE":"Q1","NAME":"","TYPE_ID"2,"DISPLAY_ORDER""0",answers:[
                        {
                          "ANSWER ":"Have received training or development programs in the past year."
                         },
                       { 
                            ANSWER: Have not had any formal education/training.
                           }
                      ]
                    },  
                   {"code": Q3, name : How do you rate your current job performance?, type_id 1,"display_order"2",answers:[
                        {
                          "ANSWER ":"Excellent"
                         } ,{"answer":"Good"}, 
                       { ANSWER: Fair},{ answer:"Poor"}
                      ]
                    },  
                   {"code": Q4, name : What do you think are the most important skills for your job?, type_id 1,"display_order"3",answers:[
                        {
                          "ANSWER ":"Communication"
                         } ,{"answer":"Problem-solving"}, 
                       { ANSWER: Leadership},{ answer:"Time management"}
                      ]
                    },  
                   {"code": Q5, name : What do you think is the most effective way to improve your job performance?, type_id 1,"display_order"4",answers:[
                        {
                          "ANSWER ":"Training and development programs"
                         } ,{"answer":"Mentoring"}, 
                       { ANSWER: Feedback},{ answer:"Autonomy"}
                      ]
                    },  
                   {"code": Q6, name : Would you recommend our training or developmental program to your colleagues?, type_id 1,"display_order"5",answers:[
                        {
                          "ANSWER ":"Yes"
                         } ,{"answer":"No"}, 
                       { ANSWER: Maybe}
                     ]}]}]
```

Here is the generated Questionnaire in JSON format:
```

{
"data" : 
{  
   "_TF_QUESTIONS":[
      {   
         "__CODE__":"Q1",
          "__NAME__":
             {"en": "Have you participated in any training or development programs within your organization during this quarter?"},
            __TYPE_ID__: 2,
           _DISPLAY_ORDER_:0,            
        },
       {
        
"ANSWERS":
[
   {"_Answer_" :{"value":"Yes","label":{"en":""}},
    "_Comment__":null
}
,{
"value":"",
"label":{"en":"","commentary"}
}

],
      "__CODE__":
         "Q1",
          __NAME__':
             { 
                en: Have you participated in any training or development programs within your organization during this quarter?
              },
            _TYPE_ID_:2,
           DISPLAY_ORDER_ :0,            
        }
       ],
"__TF_QUESTIONNAIRES__[{
  "__CODE__":
    "TRAININGDEV",
   __NAME__':
      {"en":Training and Development Programs},
     TYPE_ID:3
}]

```

Here are the details of each question:

1. Have you participated in any training or development programs within your organization during this quarter? (Multiple Choice)

This is a multiple-choice type, where respondents can choose one answer from several options.

2. What was most valuable about these trainings/development program(s)?

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100054
     - Topic: WorkLife Balance
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance with 7 questions

-------------------
-------------------

                {
                    "CODE":"WLWLB001",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "TYPE_ID":3,
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[
                        {"code":"","name","type_id",answers}
                    ]
                }
            ]

```

{

                     _TYPE_ID_: 3,
                      __QUESTIONS__":
                        [{
                            '_code_' :'Q1',

                             'What tools or software do you use to manage your workload?',
                               "_type_id_":1,
                                "__answers__":

{

        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":

                {
                    "CODE":"WORKPLACE_CULTURE",
                    "NAME":"",
                    "TYPE_ID":3,
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[

                        // Question: How would you rate the overall work environment in your team?
                        {" CODE ":"Q1", 
                         " NAME ":"
How do I feel about my workplace culture? (Scale 5-10, where 8 is neutral and above that means positive.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'Very Positive' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        // Question What are the most important values for you in your work environment?
                        {" CODE ":"Q2", 
                         " NAME ":"
What matters to me when it comes to my workplace culture? (Select all that apply.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'Collaboration' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        
                       // Question What do you think is the biggest strength of your team's work environment?
                        {" CODE ":"Q3", 
                         " NAME ":"
What makes my workplace culture so great? (Select all that apply.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'Open Communication' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        
                       // Question What do you think is the biggest area for improvement in your team's work environment?
                        {" CODE ":"Q4", 
                         " NAME ":"
What could my workplace culture improve on? (Select all that apply.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'More Recognition' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        
                       // Question How often do you feel recognized and appreciated by your team members?
                        {" CODE ":"Q5", 
                         " NAME ":"
How valued I am in my workplace culture? (Scale 1-10, where above that means positive.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'Very Often' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        
                       // Question How do you think your team's work environment compares to others?
                        {" CODE ":"Q6", 
                         " NAME ":"
How does my workplace culture compare? (Select all that apply.)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: 'Better than Most' },
                                  
                              ]
                           },

                        
                       // Question What would you like your team's work environment to be in the future?
                        {" CODE ":"Q7", 
                         " NAME ":"
What I wish my workplace culture could become? (Open-ended text)",
                          "_TF_ANSWERS":
                            [
                                { ANSWER: '' }
                              ]
                           }

                    ]

                }],

}
