Here is the generated questionnaire on Workplace Culture with 8 questions:

```json
{
    "data": {
        "_TF_QUESTIONNAIRES":
            [
                {
                  "CODE":"WORKPLACE_CULTURE",
                   "NAME":"",
                	"TYPE_ID":3,
                    "_TF_QUESTIONS":[

                        // Question: Do you feel valued and recognized for your contributions to the team?
                        {"code":"VALUED_CONTRIBUTION","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":0,["_tf_answers":[{"answer":""},{"answer":"+ I always receive recognition when due."},{"answer":- "I don't think my efforts are noticed at all"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you feel comfortable sharing your ideas and opinions with colleagues?
                        {"code":"IDEA_SHARING","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":2,["_tf_answers":[{"answer":""},{"answer":"+ I always share new thoughts."},{"answer":- "I rarely speak up"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you feel like the company prioritizes employee well-being and mental health?
                        {"code":"WELL_BEING","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":4,["_tf_answers":[{"answer":""},{"answer":"+ I think it's a top priority."},{"answer":- "I don't know if they really care"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you feel like the company values diversity and inclusion?
                        {"code":"DIVERSITY_INCLUSION","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":6,["_tf_answers":[{"answer":""},{"answer":"+ I think it's a core value."},{"answer":- "I don't see much effort to promote inclusivity"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: How would you rate the overall morale of your team?
                        {"code":"TEAM_MORALE","name":"","type_id":3,"display_order":8,["_tf_answers":[{"value":""},{"value":"+ Excellent - We're all motivated and engaged."},{"answer":- "Poor - Morale is low"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you feel like the company provides adequate support for your professional development?
                        {"code":"PROFESSIONAL_DEVELOPMENT","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":10,["_tf_answers":[{"value":""},{"answe":"+ I always have opportunities to grow."},{"answer":- "I don't see any training or mentorship"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you feel like the company fosters a sense of community and camaraderie among employees?
                        {"code":"COMMUNITY_CAMARADERIE","name":"","type_id":1,"display_order":12,["_tf_answers":[{"value":""},{"answer":"+ I think we're all close friends."},{"answe":- "I don't feel like part of the team"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: Do you have any suggestions for improving workplace culture?
                        {"code":"SUGGESTIONS","name":"","type_id":4,"display_order":14,["_tf_answers":[{"value":""},{"answer":"+ I think we should offer more flexible work arrangements."},{"answe":- "I don't know what would improve things"}]}],

                        
                         // Question: How satisfied are you with the overall workplace culture?
                        {"code":"SATISFACTION","name":"","type_id":3,"display_order":16,["_tf_answers":[{"value":""},{"answer":"+ Extremely Satisfied - I love my job."},{"answe":- "Not at All Satisfaction"}]}],

                    ]
                }
            ]

    }

}
```

This questionnaire is designed to assess the respondent's perception of workplace culture. It covers various aspects such as feeling valued, sharing ideas and opinions with colleagues, prioritizing employee well-being, valuing diversity & inclusion, team morale, professional development support, fostering community camaraderie among employees, suggestions for improving work place culture, satisfaction level.

Please note that this is just a sample questionnaire structure in JSON format.
